CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "auth_group_permissions" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "group_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_group" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "permission_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_permission" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "auth_user_groups" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "user_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "group_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_group" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_memcomment" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "comment" text NOT NULL, "date" datetime NOT NULL, "membrane_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membranetopol" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "user_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_membranetopol_prot" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "membranetopol_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membranetopol" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "membraneprot_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membraneprot" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_membranetopol_reference" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "membranetopol_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membranetopol" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "reference_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "homepage_reference" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS "membranes_membranetopol" ("id" integer NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, "name" varchar(100) NOT NULL, "temperature" integer unsigned NOT NULL CHECK ("temperature" >= 0), "equilibration" integer unsigned NOT NULL CHECK ("equilibration" >= 0), "mem_file" varchar(100) NULL, "compo_file" varchar(100) NULL, "other_file" varchar(100) NULL, "nb_lipids" integer unsigned NULL CHECK ("nb_lipids" >= 0), "description" text NOT NULL, "date" date NOT NULL, "curator_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "auth_user" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "forcefield_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "forcefields_forcefield" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "membrane_id" integer NULL REFERENCES "membranes_membrane" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED, "software_id" integer NOT NULL REFERENCES "forcefields_software" ("id") DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED);
